< Review>
Looking back, I realize that BC is one of the best Community Colleges in CA. Yes, it's imperfect. But there is opportunity here for those who aren't quite sure what path they want to follow. I was the first in my family to ever attend college. I wasn't ready, but BC allowed me to learn how to study, to prepare for the rigors of four-year college. Most of the classes I took here transferred to the Univ. of CA, where I finished my B.S. in 5.5 years total. After that, I earned my doctorate from the Univ. of Arizona and did cancer research. My point is: it's okay to "start small", because it's where your journey takes you that really matters.</Review>

< Review>
It's my first and only college so far but this place has been great. I am one class away from graduating and could not have done it if not for the amazing scholarship and financial aid opportunities provided through FASFA, the college, and local sponsors. The professors are great for the most part and the online class options work wonderfully around my hectic work schedule. The campus is very large and parking can mean a long walk. Only concern is safety due to the surrounding areas and increased crime in our city, but the school promptly notifies students by email of local reported incidents on and off campus to keep you informed. I'm so glad I chose this school as my first college. Thank you BC!<//Review>

<Text>My experienced started when a CBX roof inspector arrived at my home and explained that my residence is located in an area that had experienced a severe hail storm.   The inspector told me that other homes in my area had experienced roof damage from this storm.  The inspector offered to inspect my roof for free, so I agreed to the inspection.  When the CBX inspector came back down from the roof he explained that he had located hail damage.  The CBX inspector suggested that I contact my insurance company regarding my hail damaged roof.

After a period of time had passed another CBX agent met with my insurance claims agent and they inspected my roof together.  Both men agreed that hail damage was evident on my roof, so the insurance claims agent started the approval process to replace my entire roof.

This week a CBX crew along with their supervisor, Robert Wessely replaced my roof.  The work performed by the roof crew was excellent.  The crew was extremely well organized,  and they were friendly.  Supervisor Wessely was excellent at coordinating the effort.  And he kept me informed of what to expect throughout the process.

I recommend CBX Roofing to everyone in and around Redding. When David from CBX arrived at my house in early December we were supposed to have our roof completed within a few days. But then a series of unfortunate and unforeseen events ensued that kept the project from being completed until mid-January. So how does CBX rate so highly on a project that took longer than originally expected? I could go on and on about how great our experience with CBX was, but I will keep it to three main reasons.

First, when the old roof was removed they found a dangerous configuration of illegal wiring that had been installed many years ago by the previous homeowner. CBX worked with the city on our behalf to ensure that the future design was up to code and, more importantly, safe for my family. They also coordinated with our insurance company to get an electrician to bid the project as quickly as possible. But then the rains came. For those of you in this part of the country, you understand our rainy season is quite unpredictable but pretty consistently wet through December and January. We knew we would be roofless for much longer than we wanted. We were nervous, but this was the second time that CBX rose to the occasion. David and team sprang into action and made sure our roof was tarped to protect us from the crazy wind and rain we experienced over the course of 3-4 weeks. During that time we had a couple of leaks (water always finds a way in), but each time it happened David was onsite to readjust or add a layer of tarp to prevent any actual damage, one time even at 6:45 on a Sunday morning. But the CBX team didn‚Äôt stop there. The third house-saving/money-saving/life-saving/marriage-saving moment came when the CBX office went to bat for us with our insurance claim. They fought for us and ended up saving us thousands of dollars because of their understanding of claims, codes, and the overall insurance process.

This could have been a nightmare experience, but with CBX it was merely a little bump in the road. The entire team we interacted with: Dan, Bob, Ron, McNeal, and Jeremy to name a few‚Ä¶ everyone involved was friendly, professional, hard-working, and helpful. If you want someone to make sure that your roof not only gets done right, but also that you will have an excellent experience from start to finish, then call CBX. I am sure all of the Project Managers are great there, too, but if I were you I would specifically ask for David. For us he was the difference. He kept us informed, he was always accessible (sorry for all the calls and texts, David), and he even made sure my children kept their distance from any nails on the ground (which his team soon picked once they got off the roof!).</review>

We had CBX replace our roof after a hail storm here in town. They were very responsive at the beginning when they were trying to acquire our business. After we signed the contract it all changed. I had called several times to get the schedule date and did not have anyone call me back after several calls. When I finally heard from them and received a date, we scheduled a few days before I left for vacation so that I could be home for the project. I had a large dog that would not have behaved well with them working and I wanted to be there to keep the dog from barking etc. They call me a couple of days before the start date and they had to push the project back. I wasn't happy but I understood. They completed the project within a few days. It took several weeks for the final inspection to come back. When they finally charged me it was much more than the original insurance approved amount. The original quote was $14,000 and the final bill was $21,000. My insurance ended up not covering all of it and money I was given for other hail damage repairs went to the roof bill. I was trying to work out the details with my insurance company to see if they would cover more as I was having to pay more than my deductible. Suddenly I heard from CBX all the time requesting payment. When I needed to get ahold of someone I never heard anything but when money was due they were contacting me often. I had a small portion of the final bill that was due after insurance basically told me I should have shopped around for pricing. I sent an email to the bill employee after I made a partial payment that I would pay the remaining balance in a few weeks. She said that was great. About a week later I get a notice in the mail that a lien was placed on my house. No warning at all. I could have found a way to pay this had I known this was going to be happening. My parents who had 2 roofs done by them received a lien as well around the same time frame. It understand the need to collect payment but I feel the customer service was lacking the entire time. A little notice would have been great. I highly recommend anyone looking to get a roof done by cbx to weigh other options. I know other people that had good quality roofs done with less headaches for much cheaper.< /Text>

Review # 1 (first impression)
Put in a request for an inspection and was answered by Parker in less than 24 hours, set up the appointment easily. Parker was on time and answered my questions to my satisfaction about the process,  how they work with city inspections, what type of code requirements I can expect  and what my out of pocket expenses would be. I am happy that CBX will take the whole project on, working with my insurance and getting my roof replaced.

Review #2 (Job well done)
So now it is April 2020 and the roof is finished.  I was told that due to the backlog of roofing jobs in my area and weather it would take this long to get it done so no problem with the wait, also having someone from CBX touching base with me from time to time really helped me know they were working towards getting the job done.

David, my project manager made sure I knew what to expect, kept me informed as to the timeline / process and made sure I was informed as the project progressed. Naturally there were some issues with my roof, rotten sheathing, repairs to be done. These issues were handled quickly and professionally. David called and explained the issues prior to the repairs without trying to pressure me into additional expenses and worked with me along the way. David gained my trust by overseeing the completion of the job and making sure it was a quality job. < Review>
CAUTION:  If you have the Open Eave type of roof structure common in Redding,  CBX uses staples that penetrate completely through the wood causing splinters making repair and repaint necessary!!

This was not a problem with our original roofing.

CBX completed our 4800 sq ft hail damaged roof in approximately two days.

Reroofing with shingles makes a huge mess, but our property was cleaned beyond expectation at the end of the job.

The crew worked through 107 degree temps and spent very little time off the roof at at their beverage cooler.  The quality of the job almost met our expectation plus some and incorporated the new code requirements.

The cost was less than other local contractors and CBX handled the cost of the claim with our insurance company.  Painless for the homeowner.<//Review>

<Rate>5</Rate>< text>
Smaller version of the Blue Bottle on University, but equally great coffee and liege waffles (yum!). The ambiance is clean and sleek, and the service is fast and nice.

The avocado toast was also super fresh, a little more on the citric side, but the seeded toast itself was delicious.

They also offer alternative milks like Oat (Oatly), almond and soy milks.</text>
